# Memoric Tool Reference

Generated from the runtime `tools/list`, `resources/list`, and `resources/templates/list` surfaces. Do not hand-edit this file.

- Generated: `deterministic-runtime-tools-list`
- Source: `cargo run --quiet` -> `initialize` -> `tools/list` + `resources/list` + `resources/templates/list`
- Tool count: `12`
- Resource count: `13`
- Resource template count: `4`
- Drift gate coverage: `annotations`, `_meta.ui.resourceUri`, display metadata, `execution`, action policy traits, parameter aliases, redaction classification, input/output schemas, resources, and resource templates

## Tool Index

- [`memoric`](#memoric)
  - CALL THIS FIRST. Memory weapon guide & workflow assistant. Returns available capabilities, suggests optimal attack workflows, and shows current session status.
- [`target`](#target)
  - [TARGET] Process/thread/module operations. List/find processes, enumerate threads, list loaded DLLs, suspend/resume threads, get thread context (RIP/RSP/RAX-R15).
- [`memory`](#memory)
  - [MEMORY] Memory read/write/scan/query plus guarded allocation, protection changes, scan sessions, and read-only diagnostics.
- [`inject`](#inject)
  - [INJECT] Authorized lab injection workflows, process hollowing variants, and thread hijacking helpers.
- [`payload`](#payload)
  - [PAYLOAD] Payload utilities: PE parsing (imports/exports/sections/IAT), obfuscation (XOR/RC4/AES-256-CTR/polymorphic/UUID/IPv4/MAC), serialization, and injection lifecycle control.
- [`hook`](#hook)
  - [HOOK] Function hooking: IAT patching, inline detours (JMP), and hardware breakpoints (DR0-DR3, invisible to memory integrity checks). Also supports hook removal.
- [`stealth`](#stealth)
  - [STEALTH] Defensive posture review plus explicitly authorized evasion lab actions for telemetry, syscall, module, and policy surfaces.
- [`detect`](#detect)
  - [DETECT] EDR, hook, ETW, VM/sandbox, integrity, and forensic-tool checks.
- [`privilege`](#privilege)
  - [PRIVILEGE] Privilege posture checks, token review, SeDebug handling, and policy-gated elevation workflows.
- [`kernel`](#kernel)
  - [KERNEL] Driver/BYOVD operations, kernel memory, callbacks, ETW, PPL, DKOM, and other policy-gated kernel workflows.
- [`self`](#self)
  - [SELF] Self introspection: read PEB, query heap info, memory self-test, and self-protection operations.
- [`orchestrate`](#orchestrate)
  - [ORCHESTRATE] Static planning, safe templates, environment assessment, and explicitly opted-in chain execution.

## Resource Index

| URI | Name | MIME Type | Description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `memoric://status` | Server Status | `application/json` | Current memoric server status, privilege level, and capabilities |
| `memoric://capabilities` | Capabilities | `application/json` | Runtime readiness, policy, and action registry summary |
| `memoric://policy` | Policy | `application/json` | Current policy level and audit configuration |
| `memoric://tasks` | Tasks | `application/json` | Process-local MCP task registry |
| `memoric://audit/recent` | Recent Audit | `application/json` | Recent JSONL audit entries when MEMORIC_AUDIT_PATH is configured |
| `memoric://artifacts` | Artifact Registry | `application/json` | Process-local artifact resource links with retention and integrity metadata |
| `memoric://timeline` | Observability Timeline | `application/json` | Read-only timeline linking MCP requests, tasks, audit entries, worker IPC, and artifacts by correlation ID |
| `ui://memoric/dashboard` | Memoric Dashboard UI Data | `text/html;profile=mcp-app` | Read-only MCP Apps dashboard hydration data for tasks, policy, audit, capabilities, artifacts, and timeline |
| `ui://memoric/scans` | Memoric Scan Explorer UI Data | `text/html;profile=mcp-app` | Read-only MCP Apps scan explorer hydration data with bounded scan session and candidate pages |
| `ui://memoric/plans` | Memoric Plan Review UI Data | `text/html;profile=mcp-app` | Read-only MCP Apps plan review hydration data for dry-run plans, templates, blocked steps, and capability blockers |
| `memoric://processes` | Process List | `application/json` | Running processes on the target system |
| `memoric://scan-sessions` | Scan Sessions | `application/json` | Active memory scan sessions |
| `memoric://drivers` | Loaded Drivers | `application/json` | Available BYOVD drivers and their status |

## Resource Template Index

| URI Template | Name | MIME Type | Description |
|---|---|---|---|
| `ui://memoric/dashboard{?limit,correlation_id}` | Memoric Dashboard | `text/html;profile=mcp-app` | Read-only operation dashboard for task status, policy, audit, capability readiness, artifacts, and timeline context |
| `ui://memoric/scans{?session_id,limit,offset,cursor,sort,summary_only}` | Memoric Scan Explorer | `text/html;profile=mcp-app` | Read-only scan session explorer with bounded pagination and strict default redaction |
| `ui://memoric/plans{?template,limit,offset,cursor,dry_run}` | Memoric Plan Review | `text/html;profile=mcp-app` | Read-only orchestration plan review for effective plans, blocked steps, policy decisions, templates, and capability blockers |
| `memoric://artifact/sha256/{sha256}` | Artifact By SHA-256 | `application/octet-stream` | Retention-bound artifact resource content with SHA-256 verification |

## memoric

CALL THIS FIRST. Memory weapon guide & workflow assistant. Returns available capabilities, suggests optimal attack workflows, and shows current session status.

- Property count: `12`
- Required fields: `none`
- Read-only hint: `True`
- Destructive hint: `False`
- Highest policy: `observe`
- Display title: `Guide`
- Icon hint: `compass`
- Selection hint: Start here for action discovery, server status, and domain-specific guides.
- Output required fields: `success, code`
- Task support: `optional`
- UI resource: `ui://memoric/dashboard`
- UI visibility: `user`
- Data classifications: `artifact-reference, local-sensitive, public`

### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Default | Bounds | Description | Enum |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `allow_protected_target` | `boolean` | no | `false` | `` | Explicit override for state-changing operations against protected or critical Windows targets |  |
| `artifact_retention_secs` | `integer` | no | `900` | `>= 1; <= 86400` | Retention window for process-local artifact resource links emitted by this call; values outside the registry bounds are rejected before dispatch |  |
| `as_task` | `boolean` | no | `false` | `` | Compatibility flag for task-augmented execution: run eligible read-only or dry-run calls in the process-local MCP task registry for polling/cancellation. MCP clients may prefer params.task. |  |
| `domain` | `string` | no | `` | `` | Show detailed help for a specific domain | target, memory, inject, payload, hook, stealth, detect, privilege, kernel, self, orchestrate, all |
| `dry_run` | `boolean` | no | `false` | `` | Preview a state-changing operation without executing it where supported |  |
| `goal` | `string` | no | `` | `` | Describe your objective for workflow suggestions (e.g. 'inject shellcode stealthily') |  |
| `purpose` | `string` | no | `` | `` | Caller-provided authorized purpose for audit/provenance |  |
| `redaction` | `string` | no | `"standard"` | `` | Result redaction profile. strict suppresses raw bytes, hex blobs, credential-like fields, and paths from inline output. | none, standard, strict |
| `request_id` | `string` | no | `` | `` | Optional caller request ID for audit/provenance |  |
| `status` | `boolean` | no | `false` | `` | Show current session state |  |
| `task_id` | `string` | no | `` | `` | Task ID propagated to long-running handlers for cooperative cancellation |  |
| `timeout_ms` | `integer` | no | `600000` | `>= 1; <= 3600000` | Per-call cooperative timeout in milliseconds; long-running handlers check it at safe boundaries |  |

## target

[TARGET] Process/thread/module operations. List/find processes, enumerate threads, list loaded DLLs, suspend/resume threads, get thread context (RIP/RSP/RAX-R15).

- Property count: `30`
- Required fields: `action`
- Read-only hint: `False`
- Destructive hint: `False`
- Highest policy: `lab-write`
- Display title: `Target Inspection`
- Icon hint: `crosshair`
- Selection hint: Use for read-only process, module, thread, handle, and string inspection.
- Output required fields: `success, code`
- Task support: `optional`
- Data classifications: `artifact-reference, credential-like, local-sensitive, path, public, raw-memory`

## memory

[MEMORY] Memory read/write/scan/query plus guarded allocation, protection changes, scan sessions, and read-only diagnostics.

- Property count: `71`
- Required fields: `action`
- Read-only hint: `False`
- Destructive hint: `False`
- Highest policy: `lab-write`
- Display title: `Memory Operations`
- Icon hint: `binary`
- Selection hint: Use for authorized memory reads, scans, diagnostics, and guarded write previews.
- Output required fields: `success, code`
- Task support: `optional`
- UI resource: `ui://memoric/scans`
- UI visibility: `user`
- Data classifications: `artifact-reference, local-sensitive, path, public, raw-memory`

### Actions

`read`, `typed_read`, `write`, `typed_write`, `write_string`, `scan`, `query`, `query_find`, `alloc`, `free`, `protect`, `scan_new`, `scan_next`, `scan_undo`, `scan_list`, `scan_reset`, `scan_freeze`, `diagnostics`

| Field | Type | Required | Default | Bounds | Description | Enum |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `action` | `string` | yes | `` | `` | Memory operation to perform. typed_read/typed_write handle primitive numeric values with endian and alignment metadata. write_string/query_find are explicit AI-friendly aliases for string writes and filtered region lookups. scan_new/scan_next/scan_undo/scan_list/scan_reset/scan_freeze = Cheat Engine-style persistent scan workflow. diagnostics = read-only defensive memory layout/profile summary. | read, typed_read, write, typed_write, write_string, scan, query, query_find, alloc, free, protect, scan_new, scan_next, scan_undo, scan_list, scan_reset, scan_freeze, diagnostics |
| `address` | `integer \| string` | no | `` | `` | Memory address (int or hex string '0x1234') |  |

## inject

[INJECT] Authorized lab injection workflows, process hollowing variants, and thread hijacking helpers.

- Property count: `28`
- Required fields: `action`
- Read-only hint: `False`
- Destructive hint: `False`
- Highest policy: `privileged`
- Display title: `Injection Workflows`
- Icon hint: `send`
- Selection hint: Use only for explicitly authorized lab injection workflows and previews.
- Output required fields: `success, code`
- Task support: `optional`
- Data classifications: `artifact-reference, local-sensitive, public, raw-memory`

### Actions

`shellcode`, `dll`, `spawn`, `hijack_enum`, `hijack_backup`, `hijack_redirect`, `hijack_restore`, `hijack_wait`, `create_remote_thread`, `nt_create_thread`, `fiber`, `threadpool`, `stack_bomb`, `pool_party_worker`, `pool_party_work`, `pool_party_direct`, `pool_party_timer`, `export_forward`, `phantom_hollow`, `transacted_hollow`, `wow64_detect`

### Data Classification

| Output Path | Classification |
|---|---|
| `artifacts[].kind` | `public` |
| `artifacts[].path` | `artifact-reference` |
| `artifacts[].uri` | `artifact-reference` |
| `artifacts[].name` | `public` |
| `artifacts[].mimeType` | `public` |
| `artifacts[].size_bytes` | `public` |
| `artifacts[].sha256` | `public` |

## payload

[PAYLOAD] Payload utilities: PE parsing (imports/exports/sections/IAT), obfuscation (XOR/RC4/AES-256-CTR/polymorphic/UUID/IPv4/MAC), serialization, and injection lifecycle control.

- Property count: `34`
- Required fields: `action`
- Read-only hint: `False`
- Destructive hint: `False`
- Highest policy: `lab-write`
- Display title: `Payload Utilities`
- Icon hint: `package`
- Selection hint: Use for payload parsing, obfuscation, serialization, and lifecycle helpers.
- Output required fields: `success, code`
- Task support: `optional`
- Data classifications: `artifact-reference, local-sensitive, public, raw-memory`

### Actions

`pe_parse`, `obfuscate`, `wait`, `exit_code`, `cleanup`, `serialize`

## hook

[HOOK] Function hooking: IAT patching, inline detours (JMP), and hardware breakpoints (DR0-DR3, invisible to memory integrity checks). Also supports hook removal.

- Property count: `28`
- Required fields: `action`
- Read-only hint: `False`
- Destructive hint: `False`
- Highest policy: `privileged`
- Display title: `Hook Management`
- Icon hint: `plug`
- Selection hint: Use for hook install, remove, restore, and trampoline workflows.
- Output required fields: `success, code`
- Task support: `optional`
- Data classifications: `artifact-reference, local-sensitive, path, public, raw-memory`

### Actions

`hook_function`, `install`, `install_iat`, `remove`, `remove_iat`, `install_hwbp`, `remove_hwbp`, `trampoline`, `detour`, `restore`, `winhook`, `hwbp_syscall`

## stealth

[STEALTH] Defensive posture review plus explicitly authorized evasion lab actions for telemetry, syscall, module, and policy surfaces.

- Property count: `77`
- Required fields: `action`
- Read-only hint: `False`
- Destructive hint: `True`
- Highest policy: `destructive`
- Display title: `Stealth Controls`
- Icon hint: `shield`
- Selection hint: Use for defensive posture review or explicitly authorized evasion lab actions.
- Output required fields: `success, code`
- Task support: `optional`
- Data classifications: `artifact-reference, local-sensitive, public, raw-memory`

### Actions

`patch_etw`, `patch_amsi`, `patch_cfg`, `patch_cig`, `unhook_ntdll`, `unhook_function`, `hide_module`, `fluctuate_module`, `module_stomp`, `sleep_ekko`, `sleep_foliage`, `sleep_gargoyle`, `sleep_death`, `spoof_callstack`, `spoof_ppid`, `spoof_return`, `deep_stack_spoof`, `syscall_write`, `syscall_alloc`, `syscall_protect`, `syscall_thread`, `syscall_open`, `syscall_read`, `syscall_query`, `syscall_close`, `syscall_free`, `syscall_stealth_read`, `syscall_inject`, `encrypt_memory`, `decrypt_memory`, `mutate_code`, `sysmon_blind`, `timestomp`, `etw_provider_disable`, `etw_mass_disable`, `create_suspended`, `testsign_hide_ntquery`, `testsign_hide_self`, `testsign_hide_bcd`, `testsign_query`, `testsign_auto_inject`, `testsign_launch_hooked`, `testsign_kernel_bypass`, `testsign_launch_clean`, `testsign_ci_callback`, `testsign_ci_func_patch`, `testsign_pte_rw`, `wdac_disable`, `wdac_restore`, `defender_disable`, `defender_restore`, `defender_status`, `defender_add_exclusion`, `defender_mpcmdrun`, `firewall_add_rule`, `firewall_remove_rule`, `firewall_list_rules`, `firewall_disable`, `firewall_enable`, `firewall_status`, `sentinel_start`, `sentinel_stop`, `sentinel_status`, `sentinel_self_destruct`, `callback_enum_by_driver`, `callback_masquerade`, `etw_ti_selective_disable`, `minifilter_enum_classified`, `minifilter_selective_detach`, `minifilter_pause`, `minifilter_resume`

## detect

[DETECT] EDR, hook, ETW, VM/sandbox, integrity, and forensic-tool checks.

- Property count: `15`
- Required fields: `action`
- Read-only hint: `False`
- Destructive hint: `False`
- Highest policy: `privileged`
- Display title: `Detection Review`
- Icon hint: `radar`
- Selection hint: Use for EDR, telemetry, sandbox, integrity, and environment checks.
- Output required fields: `success, code`
- Task support: `optional`
- Data classifications: `artifact-reference, credential-like, local-sensitive, path, public, raw-memory`

### Actions

`edr_products`, `edr_hooks`, `edr_quick_check`, `edr_suspend`, `etw_sessions`, `veh_chain`, `vm_sandbox`, `hypervisor`, `forensics`, `integrity`, `hooks`, `hook_function`, `syscall_resolve`, `stealth_score`, `bypass_recommendations`

## privilege

[PRIVILEGE] Privilege posture checks, token review, SeDebug handling, and policy-gated elevation workflows.

- Property count: `20`
- Required fields: `action`
- Read-only hint: `False`
- Destructive hint: `False`
- Highest policy: `privileged`
- Display title: `Privilege Review`
- Icon hint: `key`
- Selection hint: Use for privilege posture, token review, and authorized elevation workflows.
- Output required fields: `success, code`
- Task support: `optional`
- Data classifications: `artifact-reference, credential-like, local-sensitive, path, public, raw-memory`

## kernel

- Property count: `161`
- Required fields: `action`
- Read-only hint: `False`
- Destructive hint: `True`
- Highest policy: `destructive`
- Display title: `Kernel Driver`

- Output required fields: `success, code`
- Task support: `optional`
- Data classifications: `artifact-reference, credential-like, local-sensitive, path, public, raw-memory`

### Actions

| `driver_kernel_apc` | `False` | `True` | `True` | `True` | `False` | `critical` | `kernel` | `pid` | `pid`: `pid_u32` | `tid`, `shellcode_size`, `shellcode_addr` when `apc_action` is `inject` default applies Kernel APC shellcode injection requires the target thread ID, shellcode size, and shellcode address.; `tid`, `dll_path` when `apc_action` is `dll` Kernel APC DLL injection requires the target thread ID and DLL path. |  |  | `administrator`: Administrative rights are required for kernel-backed operations; `kernel driver access`: A reachable kernel driver or equivalent approved capability is required; `capability preflight`: Capability checks must confirm that the selected kernel path is available | `kernel driver, kernel memory, or system state mutation`: Kernel workflow may load drivers or alter kernel/system state | `driver`: memoric driver device access `operation-specific IOCTL access` | available `action-dependent`; strategy `driver_captured_original_state`; captures `driver_state`, `original_state`, `target`; kernel rollback requires driver support and captured original state | `thread_id` -> `tid` | `apc_action`: `inject`, `dll` |  | `shellcode_size`: >= `1`; <= `4194304` | `apc_action`: `string` choices `inject`, `dll`; `dll_path`: `path`; `pid`: `pid_u32`; `shellcode_addr`: `address_u64`; `shellcode_size`: `u64` >= `1`; <= `4194304`; `thread_id`: `tid_u32` aliases `thread_id`; `tid`: `tid_u32` aliases `thread_id` | `artifact-reference, credential-like, local-sensitive, path, public, raw-memory` |
| `driver_wfp_remove` | `False` | `True` | `True` | `True` | `False` | `critical` | `kernel` |  |  | `callout_id` when `wfp_action` is `remove` WFP single-remove requires the target callout ID; enum and nuke modes can omit a single callout target. |  |  | `administrator`: Administrative rights are required for kernel-backed operations; `kernel driver access`: A reachable kernel driver or equivalent approved capability is required; `capability preflight`: Capability checks must confirm that the selected kernel path is available | `kernel driver, kernel memory, or system state mutation`: Kernel workflow may load drivers or alter kernel/system state | `driver`: memoric driver device access `operation-specific IOCTL access` | available `action-dependent`; strategy `driver_captured_original_state`; captures `driver_state`, `original_state`, `target`; kernel rollback requires driver support and captured original state | `provider` -> `provider_name` | `wfp_action`: `enum`, `remove`, `nuke` |  |  | `callout_id`: `u64`; `provider`: `string` aliases `provider`; `provider_name`: `string` aliases `provider`; `wfp_action`: `string` choices `enum`, `remove`, `nuke` | `artifact-reference, credential-like, local-sensitive, path, public, raw-memory` |

| `action` | `string` | yes | `` | `` | Kernel action. Groups: read-only status/readiness, generic helpers (driver_load/read/pte_modify/etc), hybrid actions (ppl_bypass/dkom_hide/token_escalate use memoric.sys unless device_path is provided), and direct memoric.sys actions (driver_*). Prefer canonical driver_* names over legacy aliases like notify_routine/reg_protect/object_hook/port_hide. | status, driver_load, driver_unload, driver_discover, driver_auto, read, write, physical_read, physical_write, pte_modify, vad_hide, sniff_start, sniff_stop, enum_callbacks, remove_callback, object_callback_enum, object_callback_remove, registry_callback_enum, registry_callback_remove, driver_notify_routine, driver_reg_protect, driver_object_hook, driver_port_hide, ppl_bypass, dse_bypass, dse_map_driver, dkom_hide, module_hide, minifilter_enum, minifilter_remove, token_escalate, etw_ti_remove, driver_enum_process, driver_module_hide, driver_thread_hide, driver_callback_enum, driver_callback_remove, driver_patch_kernel, driver_apc_inject, driver_handle_strip, driver_pe_dump, driver_set_debug_port, driver_dpc_timer, driver_token_dup, driver_stats, driver_memory_pool, driver_minifilter_enum, driver_process_dump, driver_hypervisor_detect, driver_testsign_hide, driver_global_hook, driver_auto_inject, driver_infinity_hook, driver_ci_callback_patch, driver_ci_func_patch, driver_pte_rw, driver_msr_rw, driver_cloak, driver_force_kill, driver_force_delete, driver_system_thread, driver_kernel_exec, driver_ppl_bypass, driver_cr_rw, driver_idt_rw, driver_unloaded_drv_clear, driver_token_swap, driver_process_protect, driver_keylogger, driver_reg_hide, driver_file_lock, driver_etw_blind, driver_eprocess_spoof, driver_event_log_clear, driver_cred_dump, driver_impersonate, driver_callback_nuke, driver_minifilter_detach, driver_kernel_apc, driver_wfp_remove |

| `cursor` | `string` | no | `` | `` | Opaque cursor returned in pagination.nextCursor; pass unchanged to continue plan/execute result pagination |  |
| `dry_run` | `boolean` | no | `true` | `` | If true, plan but don't execute steps |  |
| `limit` | `integer \| string` | no | `` | `>= 1; <= 100` | Maximum items returned per paginated plan/execute result section |  |
| `marker_address` | `integer \| string` | no | `` | `` | Marker address printed by the benign test target for optional read-only validation |  |
| `marker_len` | `integer \| string` | no | `28` | `` | Marker byte length for lab_validation marker read |  |
| `offset` | `integer \| string` | no | `` | `` | Pagination offset for plan/execute result sections when cursor is omitted |  |
| `output_path` | `string` | no | `` | `` | Optional artifact output path for full plan/execute results; large static plans auto-export when omitted |  |
| `pid` | `integer \| string` | no | `` | `` | Target process ID (for execute) |  |
| `purpose` | `string` | no | `` | `` | Caller-provided authorized purpose for audit/provenance |  |
| `redaction` | `string` | no | `"standard"` | `` | Result redaction profile. strict suppresses raw bytes, hex blobs, credential-like fields, and paths from inline output. | none, standard, strict |
| `request_id` | `string` | no | `` | `` | Optional caller request ID for audit/provenance |  |
| `shellcode` | `array \| string` | no | `` | `` | Hex-encoded shellcode to inject (for execute) |  |
| `skip_completed_steps` | `boolean` | no | `true` | `` | Resume hint: skip checkpoint-completed step IDs when replaying the original authorized chain request |  |
| `steps` | `array` | no | `` | `` | Custom chain steps (for plan action) |  |
| `task_id` | `string` | no | `` | `` | Task ID propagated to long-running handlers for cooperative cancellation |  |
| `template` | `string` | no | `` | `` | Registered static plan template for orchestrate(action='plan') when steps are omitted | lab_validation, memory_diagnostics, driver_readiness, reconnaissance, cleanup, privilege_review |
| `timeout_ms` | `integer` | no | `600000` | `>= 1; <= 3600000` | Per-call cooperative timeout in milliseconds; long-running handlers check it at safe boundaries |  |
